Users can easily enjoy genuine Asian calligraphy and ink wash painting with a simple and intuitive user interface imbued with the Zen spirit.\r\n\r\nThe Windows universal app version of Zen Brush 2 already supports the Surface Dial and the new Surface Pen with tilt support, providing the feeling of a real ink brush by reflecting the brush's tilt and orientation.\r\n\r\nMain Features :\r\n\r\n‚ñ†3D Ink Brush Simulation\r\nThe app includes a drawing system based on a 3D model of an East Asian ink brush.
